create or replace PROCEDURE  "BRF205_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" ( REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 
IS 

  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 


BEGIN 

insert into BRF205_MAPPING_TABLE
(foracid, cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE, SCHM_CODE,NRE_STATUS,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,BACID,SOL_ID,HNI_NETWORTH)
SELECT  ACCT_NUMBER,cust_id, ACCT_NAME,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE, GL_CODE,SCHM_CODE,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,CONSTITUTION_CODE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,BACID,SOL_ID,HNI_NETWORTH
FROM general_master_table WHERE report_date = '30-JUN-2023';
COMMIT;

insert into BRF205_MAPPING_TABLE
(FORACID, ACCT_NAME,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC)
SELECT  ACCT_NO,ACCT_NAME,CURRENCY,REPORT_DATE,AMT_LC
FROM BRF_TREASURY_MASTER_TB WHERE report_date = '30-JUN-2023';



----UPDATE QUERY

'24503', '24337')

------


create or replace PROCEDURE BRF205_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   v_report_date   date := to_date (report_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY');
BEGIN


Delete from BRF205_DETAILTABLE where REPORT_DATE = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;

--ROW102
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

SELECT  
ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE  FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = '30-jun-2023' 
AND CONSTITUTION_CODE IN 'SGOVT'
AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13101', '13201', '13206', '13215', '13216', '13217', '13220', '13241', '24301', '24311', '24312', '24313', '24319', 
'24503', '24337');


--ROW103
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

SELECT  
ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE  FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = '30-jun-2023' 
AND 
CONSTITUTION_CODE IN 'SGOVT'
AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE = '13421';



--ROW104
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

SELECT  
ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE  FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = '30-jun-2023' 
AND CONSTITUTION_CODE IN 'SGOVT'
AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13241', '13601', '13611', '13631', '13641');


--ROW107
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

SELECT  
ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE  FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = '30-jun-2023' 
AND Constitution_code IN ('CGPSU', 'SGPSU', 'QGOVT', '11401', '11403', '11404', '11405', '11406', '11407', '11408', '11409')
AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN ('13101', '13201', '13206', '13215', '13216', '13217', '13220', '13241', '24301', '24311', '24312', '24313', 
'24319', '24503', '24337');

--ROW108
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

SELECT  
ACCT_NUMBER,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,
COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE  FROM GENERAL_MASTER_TABLE  where report_date = '30-jun-2023' 
AND constitution_code IN ('CGPSU', 'SGPSU', 'QGOVT', '11401', '11403', '11404', '11405', '11406', '11407', '11408', '11409')
AND GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE IN '13421';


--ROW109
insert into BRF205_DETAILTABLE
(foracid,ACCT_NAME,CUST_ID,SCHM_CODE,SCHM_TYPE,GL_SUB_HEAD_CODE,GL_CODE,ACID,NRE_FLG,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_DATE,BACID,COUNTRY_OF_INCORP,
ACT_BALANCE_AMT_LC,CONSTITUTION_CODE)

INSERT INTO  BRF205_DETAILTABLE(foracid,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE)
SELECT ACCT_NO,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,CURRENCY FROM brf_treasury_master_tb where report_date ='30-JUN-2023' and

MERGE INTO BRF205_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT distinct   b.REPORT_LABEL_1,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM BRF205_MAPPING_TABLE b
    JOIN BRF205_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.REPORT_LABEL_1 = S.REPORT_LABEL_1
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

MERGE INTO BRF205_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT distinct  b.report_addl_criteria_1,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM BRF205_MAPPING_TABLE b
    JOIN BRF205_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.report_addl_criteria_1 = S.report_addl_criteria_1
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;


COMMIT;
END;
